After moving in, I found that the sanitary conditions of the bathroom were worrying, and the water marks on the wall had turned black. When I took a shower, I found that the floor drain had an odor and the water couldn't go down.
On the second day, the waiter knocked on the door at 8:00 a.m. and woke me up, asking me if I wanted to clean the room. This is the first time I have stayed in so many hotels.
On the morning of the 3rd day, I was woken up by a married person. The married person was next door to me, and he didn't tell us when we checked in.

The only advantage may be that the fruit plate will be delivered at night, and the haggis in the alley next to it is delicious.
